<a id="1510" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="1515" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="1522" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html" class="Module">Function</a> <a id="1531" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="1537" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="1538" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Function.html#769" class="Function Operator">_∘_</a><a id="1541" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Having proved a preservation property in the last chapter, a natural
next step would be to prove progress. That is, to prove a property
of the form

    If γ ⊢ M ↓ v, then either M is a lambda abstraction or M —→ N for some N.

Such a property would tell us that having a denotation implies either
reduction to normal form or divergence. This is indeed true, but we
can prove a much stronger property! In fact, having a denotation that
is a function value (not `⊥`) implies reduction to a lambda
abstraction (no divergence).

This stronger property, reformulated a bit, is known as _adequacy_.
That is, if a term `M` is denotationally equal to a lambda abstraction,
then `M` reduces to a lambda abstraction.

    ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)  implies M —↠ ƛ N' for some N'

Recall that `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)` is equivalent to saying that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` for some `v` and `w`. We will show that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies reduction a lambda abstraction.

It is well known that a term can reduce to a lambda abstraction using
full β reduction if and only if it can reduce to a lambda abstraction
using the call-by-name reduction strategy. So we shall prove that
`γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies that `M` halts under call-by-name evaluation,
which we define with a big-step semantics written `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c`, where
`c` is a closure (a term paired with an environment) and `γ'` is an
environment that maps variables to closures

So we will show that `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v ↦ w)` implies `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c`,
provided `γ` and `γ'` are appropriate related.  The proof will
be an induction on the derivation of `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, and to
strengthen the induction hypothesis, we will relate semantic values to
closures using a _logical relation_ `𝕍`.

The rest of this chapter is organized as follows.

* We loosen the requirement that `M` result in a function value and
  instead require that `M` result in a value that is greater than or
  equal to a function value. We establish several properties about
  being ``greater than a function''.

* We define the call-by-name big-step semantics of the lambda calculus
  and prove that it is deterministic.

* We define the logical relation `𝕍` that relates values and closures,
  and extend it to a relation on terms `𝔼` and environments `𝔾`.

* We prove the main lemma,
  that if `𝔾 γ γ'` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`.

* We prove adequacy as a corollary to the main lemma.


## The property of being greater or equal to a function

We define the following short-hand for saying that a value is
greather-than or equal to a function value.

If a value `u` is greater than a function, then an even greater value `u'`
is too.

The bottom value `⊥` is not greater than a function.

If the join of two values `u` and `u'` is greater than a function, then
at least one of them is too.

           <a id="4918" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4920" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4929" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4870" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="4931" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#419" class="Datatype Operator">⊎</a> <a id="4933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="4942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4872" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

On the other hand, if neither of `u` and `u'` is greater than a function,
then their join is also not greater than a function.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-⊔"></a><a id="5368" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5368" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="5383" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5385" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5387" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5387" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5389" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5389" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5392" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5394" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5399" class="Symbol">}</a>
               <a id="5416" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5418" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5420" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5429" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5387" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5431" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5433" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5435" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5444" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5389" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>
               <a id="5462" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5464" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5466" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5475" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5387" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5478" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5480" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5389" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5482" class="Symbol">)</a>

The converse is also true. If the join of two values is not above a
function, then neither of them is individually.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-⊔-inv"></a><a id="5761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5761" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔-inv</a> <a id="5780" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5782" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="5784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5784" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5786" class="Bound">u&#39;</a> <a id="5789" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5791" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="5796" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5798" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5800" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5802" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5811" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5812" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5784" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5814" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5786" class="Bound">u&#39;</a><a id="5818" class="Symbol">)</a>
              <a id="5834" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5836" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5847" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5784" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="5849" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="5851" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="5853" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="5862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5786" class="Bound">u&#39;</a>

The property of being greater than a function value is decidable, as
exhibited by the following function.

class="Bound">lt</a><a id="6658" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6660" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="6662" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="6664" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="6668" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6670" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6673" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6675" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="6677" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6680" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6680" class="Bound">y</a> <a id="6682" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6684" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="6687" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6688" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#5368" class="Function">not-AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="6703" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6673" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="6705" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#6680" class="Bound">y</a><a id="6706" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>


## Relating values to closures

Next we relate semantic values to closures.  The relation `𝕍` is for
closures whose term is a lambda abstraction, i.e., in weak-head normal
form (WHNF). The relation 𝔼 is for any closure. Roughly speaking,
`𝔼 v c` will hold if, when `v` is greater than a function value, `c` evaluates
to a closure `c'` in WHNF and `𝕍 v c'`. Regarding `𝕍 v c`, it will hold when
`c` is in WHNF, and if `v` is a function, the body of `c` evaluates
according to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍"></a><a id="7215" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7217" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7219" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7225" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7227" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2063" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7232" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7234" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>
<a id="𝔼"></a><a id="7238" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7238" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7240" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7242" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a> <a id="7248" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7250" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2063" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7255" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7257" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We define `𝕍` as a function from values and closures to `Set` and not as a
data type because it is mutually recursive with `𝔼` in a negative
position (to the left of an implication).  We first perform case
analysis on the term in the closure. If the term is a variable or
application, then `𝕍` is false (`Bot`). If the term is a lambda
abstraction, we define `𝕍` by recursion on the value, which we
describe below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="7702" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7704" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7704" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7706" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7707" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7712" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7713" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="7715" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7715" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="7717" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7719" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7719" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7720" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7722" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7724" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="7728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7730" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7730" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7732" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7733" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7738" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7739" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7739" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="7741" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="7743" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7743" class="Bound">M₁</a><a id="7745" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7747" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7747" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7748" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7750" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7752" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#243" class="Datatype">Bot</a>
<a id="7756" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7758" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a> <a id="7760" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7761" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7766" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7767" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7769" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7769" class="Bound">M</a><a id="7770" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7772" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7772" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7773" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7775" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7777" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#69" class="Record">⊤</a>
<a id="7779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7781" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7782" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7782" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7784" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4129" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">↦</a> <a id="7786" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7786" class="Bound">w</a><a id="7787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7789" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7790" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7795" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7796" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7798" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7798" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7799" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7801" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7801" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7802" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7804" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="7810" class="Symbol">(∀{</a><a id="7813" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7813" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7815" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7817" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2063" class="Datatype">Clos</a><a id="7821" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7823" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7238" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="7827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7782" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7829" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7813" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="7831" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7833" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="7842" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7786" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7844" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7846" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="7849" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7849" class="Bound">c&#39;</a> <a id="7852" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="7854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2063" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="7859" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a>
        <a id="7869" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7801" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="7872" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2283" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="7875" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7813" class="Bound">c</a><a id="7876" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7878" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2627" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="7880" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7798" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="7882" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2627" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="7884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7849" class="Bound">c&#39;</a>  <a id="7888" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a>  <a id="7891" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7893" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7786" class="Bound">w</a> <a id="7895" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7849" class="Bound">c&#39;</a><a id="7897" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="7899" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7901" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7902" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7902" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7904" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="7906" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7906" class="Bound">v</a><a id="7907" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7909" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7910" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7915" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7916" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7918" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7919" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7921" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7921" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7922" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7924" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7902" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="7930" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7931" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7936" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7937" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7939" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7918" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7940" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7921" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7943" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7945" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="7947" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="7949" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7906" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="7951" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7952" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="7957" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7958" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="7960" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7918" class="Bound">N</a><a id="7961" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7921" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="7964" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* If the value is `⊥`, then the result is true (`⊤`).

* If the value is a join (u ⊔ v), then the result is the pair
  (conjunction) of 𝕍 is true for both u and v.

* The important case is for a function value `v ↦ w` and closure
  `clos (ƛ N) γ`. Given any closure `c` such that `𝔼 v c`, if `w` is
  greater than a function, then `N` evaluates (with `γ` extended with `c`)
  to some closure `c'` and we have `𝕍 w c'`.


The definition of `𝔼` is straightforward. If `v` is a greater than a
function, then `M` evaluates to a closure related to `v`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8540" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7238" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="8542" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8542" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8544" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8545" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="8550" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8550" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8552" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8552" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="8554" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8556" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8558" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="8567" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8542" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8569" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8571" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">Σ[</a> <a id="8574" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8574" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8576" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">∈</a> <a id="8578" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2063" class="Datatype">Clos</a> <a id="8583" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#764" class="Function">]</a> <a id="8585" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8552" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="8588" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2627" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="8590" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8550" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="8592" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2627" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="8594" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8574" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="8596" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Product.html#1353" class="Function Operator">×</a> <a id="8598" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="8600" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8542" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="8602" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8574" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof of the main lemma is by induction on `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, so it goes
underneath lambda abstractions and must therefore reason about open
terms (terms with variables). So we must relate environments of
semantic values to environments of closures.  In the following, `𝔾`
relates `γ` to `γ'` if the corresponding values and closures are related
by `𝔼`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝔾"></a><a id="8982" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8982" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="8984" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8986" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="8988" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8988" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="8989" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="8991" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="8993" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7331" class="Function">Env</a> <a id="8997" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8988" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="8999" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9001" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2033" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9009" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8988" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9011" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9013" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a>

      <a id="9136" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8982" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9140" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9098" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9142" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9109" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9145" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9147" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7238" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="9149" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9125" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9151" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9127" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9153" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9155" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#8982" class="Function">𝔾</a> <a id="9157" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9098" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9160" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#7504" class="Function Operator">`,</a> <a id="9163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9125" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9164" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9166" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9109" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="9170" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2283" class="Function Operator">,&#39;</a> <a id="9173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9127" class="Bound">c</a><a id="9174" class="Symbol">)</a>

We need a few properties of the `𝕍` and `𝔼` relations.  The first is that
a closure in the `𝕍` relation must be in weak-head normal form.  We
define WHNF has follows.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9434" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="WHNF"></a><a id="9439" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9439" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9444" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9446" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9448" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9449" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9449" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9451" class="Bound">A</a><a id="9452" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9454" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9456" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9449" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9460" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9451" class="Bound">A</a> <a id="9462" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9464" class="PrimitiveType">Set</a> <a id="9468" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="WHNF.ƛ_"></a><a id="9476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9476" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a> <a id="9479" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9481" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="9483" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9484" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9484" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9485" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9487" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9488" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9488" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="9490" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9492" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9484" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="9496" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="9498" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9500" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9501" class="Symbol">}</a>
     <a id="9508" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9439" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9515" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9516" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9488" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9519" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The proof goes by cases on the term in the closure.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍→WHNF"></a><a id="9599" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9599" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9606" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9608" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9610" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9611" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9613" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9613" class="Bound">γ</a> <a id="9615" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9617" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2033" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="9625" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="9626" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9628" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9630" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9610" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="9634" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="9636" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a><a id="9637" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9639" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9640" class="Symbol">}</a>
       <a id="9649" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9651" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9653" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9639" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9655" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9656" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="9661" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9628" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="9663" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9613" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="9664" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9666" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9668" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9439" class="Datatype">WHNF</a> <a id="9673" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9628" class="Bound">M</a>
<a id="9675" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9599" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9682" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9683" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9685" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9687" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="9689" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9689" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9690" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9692" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9693" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9693" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9694" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9696" class="Symbol">()</a>
<a id="9699" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9599" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9706" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9707" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9709" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="9713" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9713" class="Bound">N</a><a id="9714" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9716" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9717" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9717" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9718" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9720" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="9723" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9476" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ_</a>
<a id="9728" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9599" class="Function">𝕍→WHNF</a> <a id="9735" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9736" class="Argument">M</a> <a id="9738" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9740" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9740" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="9742" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="9744" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9744" class="Bound">M</a><a id="9745" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9747" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9748" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9748" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9749" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9751" class="Symbol">()</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Next we have an introduction rule for `𝕍` that mimics the `⊔-intro`
rule. If both `u` and `v` are related to a closure `c`, then their join is
too.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="𝕍⊔-intro"></a><a id="9928" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9928" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="9937" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9939" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="9941" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9941" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9943" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9945" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9945" class="Bound">v</a><a id="9946" class="Symbol">}</a>
         <a id="9957" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9959" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9961" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9943" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="9963" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9941" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="9965" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9967" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="9969" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9945" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="9971" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9941" class="Bound">c</a>
           <a id="9984" class="Comment">---------------</a>
         <a id="10009" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10011" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10013" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10014" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9943" class="Bound">u</a> <a id="10016" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4159" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10018" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9945" class="Bound">v</a><a id="10019" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10021" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9941" class="Bound">c</a>
<a id="10023" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9928" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10032" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10038" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10039" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4186" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">`</a> <a id="10041" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10041" class="Bound">x</a><a id="10042" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10044" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10044" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10045" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10047" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="10050" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10050" class="Bound">vc</a>
<a id="10053" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9928" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10062" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10063" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10068" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10069" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10071" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10071" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10072" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10074" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10075" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10077" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10080" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10080" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10083" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10085" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="10087" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10077" class="Bound">uc</a> <a id="10090" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10092" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10080" class="Bound">vc</a> <a id="10095" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="10097" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#9928" class="Function">𝕍⊔-intro</a> <a id="10106" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10107" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10112" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10113" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10113" class="Bound">L</a> <a id="10115" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4298" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">·</a> <a id="10117" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10117" class="Bound">M</a><a id="10118" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10120" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10120" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="10121" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10123" class="Symbol">()</a> <a id="10126" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10126" class="Bound">vc</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

In a moment we prove that `𝕍` is preserved when going from a greater
value to a lesser value: if `𝕍 v c` and `v' ⊑ v`, then `𝕍 v' c`.
This property, named `𝕍-sub`, is needed by the main lemma in
the case for the `sub` rule.

To prove `𝕍-sub`, we in turn need the following property concerning
values that are not greater than a function, that is, values that are
equivalent to `⊥`. In such cases, `𝕍 v (clos (ƛ N) γ')` is trivially true.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="not-AboveFun-𝕍"></a><a id="10593" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10593" class="Function">not-AboveFun-𝕍</a> <a id="10608" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10610" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="10612" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10612" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10614" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4097" class="Datatype">Value</a><a id="10621" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10623" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10623" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10624" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10626" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10626" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a> <a id="10629" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10631" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2033" class="Function">ClosEnv</a> <a id="10639" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10623" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="10640" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10642" class="Bound">N</a> <a id="10644" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10646" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10623" class="Bound">Γ</a> <a id="10648" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#3018" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10650" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4150" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="10654" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#2694" class="InductiveConstructor">★</a> <a id="10656" class="Symbol">}</a>
    <a id="10662" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10664" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#464" class="Function Operator">¬</a> <a id="10666" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4104" class="Function">AboveFun</a> <a id="10675" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10612" class="Bound">v</a>
      <a id="10683" class="Comment">-------------------</a>
    <a id="10707" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10709" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="10711" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10612" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="10713" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10714" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="10719" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10720" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="10722" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10642" class="Bound">N</a><a id="10723" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10725" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10626" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="10727" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="10729" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10593" class="Function">not-AboveFun-𝕍</a> <a id="10744" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10745" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4117" class="InductiveConstructor">⊥</a><a id="10746" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10748" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#10748" class="Bound">af</a> <a id="10751" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10753" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Unit.html#106" class="InductiveConstructor">tt</a>

The proofs of `𝕍-sub` and `𝔼-sub` are intertwined.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="sub-𝕍"></a><a id="11036" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11036" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="11042" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11044" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="11046" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11046" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11048" %}#11058" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="11060" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11062" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11064" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7215" class="Function">𝕍</a> <a id="11066" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11056" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11068" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="11075" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4468" class="Datatype Operator">⊑</a> <a id="11077" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11056" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11079" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11081" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md <a id="sub-𝔼"></a><a id="11088" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11088" class="Function">sub-𝔼</a> <a id="11094" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11096" class="Symbol">∀{</a><a id="11098" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11098" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11100" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="11102" href="{% class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="11114" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11116" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7238" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="11118" href="{% class="Bound">c</a> <a id="11122" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11124" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11110" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="11127" href="{% %}#11108" class="Bound">v</a> <a id="11131" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="11133" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#7238" class="Function">𝔼</a> <a id="11135" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11110" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="11138" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11098" class="Bound">c</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

We prove `𝕍-sub` by case analysis on the closure's term, to dispatch the
cases for variables and application. We then proceed by induction on
`v' ⊑ v`. We describe each case below.

class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="12832" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#4953" class="InductiveConstructor">Dist⊑</a> <a id="12838" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12838" class="Bound">ev1c</a> <a id="12843" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12845" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12845" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="12848" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12850" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12852" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12852" class="Bound">w&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="12856" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12858" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
    <a id="12869" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12871" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="12874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12874" class="Bound">naf2</a> <a id="12879" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12881" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.html#597" class="InductiveConstructor">no</a> <a id="12884" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12884" class="Bound">naf3</a>
    <a id="12893" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="12898" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4855" class="Function">AboveFun-⊔</a> <a id="12909" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12911" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12845" class="Bound">v&#39;</a> <a id="12914" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12916" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="12918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12852" class="Bound">w&#39;&#39;</a> <a id="12922" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12924" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12858" class="Bound">lt</a> <a id="12927" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="12929" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>
<a id="12931" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="12935" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12937" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#475" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₁</a> <a id="12942" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12942" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="12946" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12948" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="12955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12956" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="12970" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12942" class="Bound">af2</a> <a id="12974" class="Bound">naf2</a><a id="12978" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="12980" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="12984" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="12986" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Sum.Base.html#500" class="InductiveConstructor">inj₂</a> <a id="12991" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12991" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="12995" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="12997" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Data.Empty.html#360" class="Function">⊥-elim</a> <a id="13004" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13005" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Relation.Nullary.Negation.html#560" class="Function">contradiction</a> <a id="13019" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#12991" class="Bound">af3</a> <a id="13023" class="Bound">naf3</a><a id="13027" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `Bot⊑`. We immediately have `𝕍 ⊥ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `ConjL⊑`.

        v₁' ⊑ v     v₂' ⊑ v
        -------------------
        (v₁' ⊔ v₂') ⊑ v

  The induction hypotheses gives us `𝕍 v₁' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
  and `𝕍 v₂' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`, which is all we need for this case. 

* Case `ConjR1⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₁
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  The induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `ConjR2⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₂
        -------------
        v' ⊑ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)

  Again, the induction hypothesis gives us `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `Trans⊑`.

        v' ⊑ v₂   v₂ ⊑ v
        -----------------
             v' ⊑ v

  The induction hypothesis for `v₂ ⊑ v` gives us
  `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ)`. We apply the induction hypothesis
  for `v' ⊑ v₂` to conclude that `𝕍 v' (clos (ƛ N) γ)`.

* Case `Dist⊑`. This case  is the most difficult. We have

        𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)
        𝕍 (v ↦ w') (clos (ƛ N) γ)

  and need to show that 

        𝕍 (v ↦ (w ⊔ w')) (clos (ƛ N) γ)
  
  Let `c` be an arbtrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Assume `w ⊔ w'` is greater than a function.
  Unfortunately, this does not mean that both `w` and `w'`
  are above functions. But thanks to the lemma `AboveFun-⊔`,
  we know that at least one of them is greater than a function.
  
  * Suppose both of them are greater than a function.  Then we have
    `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L δ` and `𝕍 w (clos L δ)`.  We also have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ c₃` and
    `𝕍 w' c₃`.  Because the big-step semantics is deterministic, we have
    `c₃ ≡ clos L δ`. Also, from `𝕍 w (clos L δ)` we know that `L ≡ ƛ N'`
    for some `N'`. We conclude that `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') δ)`.

  * Suppose one of them is greater than a function and the other is
    not: say `AboveFun w` and `¬ AboveFun w'`. Then from
    `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ)`
    we have `γ ⊢ N ⇓ clos L γ₁` and `𝕍 w (clos L γ₁)`. From this we have
    `L ≡ ƛ N'` for some `N'`. Meanwhile, from `¬ AboveFun w'` we have
    `𝕍 w' (clos L γ₁)`. We conclude that
    `𝕍 (w ⊔ w') (clos (ƛ N') γ₁)`.
    

The proof of `sub-𝔼` is direct and explained below.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="15154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11088" class="Function">sub-𝔼</a> <a id="15160" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15161" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="15166" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15166" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="15168" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15168" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="15169" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15171" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15172" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15172" class="Bound">v</a><a id="15173" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15175" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15176" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15176" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="15178" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="15180" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15180" class="Bound">𝔼v</a> <a id="15183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15183" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="15188" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15188" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="15196" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="15201" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15180" class="Bound">𝔼v</a> <a id="15204" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15205" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4289" class="Function">AboveFun-⊑</a> <a id="15216" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15188" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="15220" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15183" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="15224" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="15226" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="15230" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="15232" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15234" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15234" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15236" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15238" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15240" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15240" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15244" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15246" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15246" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15249" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15251" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15253" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="15261" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15263" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15234" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="15265" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15267" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="15269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15240" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="15273" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="15275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11036" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="15281" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#15246" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="15284" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="15289" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="15291" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

From `AboveFun v'` and `v' ⊑ v` we have `AboveFun v`.  Then with `𝔼 v c` we
obtain a closure `c` such that `γ ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude with an
application of `sub-𝕍` with `v' ⊑ v` to show `𝕍 v' c`.


## Programs with function denotation terminate via call-by-name

The main lemma proves that if a term has a denotation that is above a
function, then it terminates via call-by-name. More formally, if
`γ ⊢ M ↓ v` and `𝔾 γ γ'`, then `𝔼 v (clos M γ')`. The proof is by
induction on the derivation of `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` we discuss each case below.

The following lemma, kth-x, is used in the case for the `var` rule.

<a id="18141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#16175" class="Function">↓→𝔼</a> <a id="18145" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18146" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18147" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18149" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18150" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="18151" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18153" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18154" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18154" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="18156" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18158" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18159" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18159" class="Bound">M</a><a id="18160" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18162" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18163" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18163" class="Bound">v&#39;</a><a id="18165" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18167" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18167" class="Bound">𝔾γγ&#39;</a> <a id="18172" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18173" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Denotational.md %}{% raw %}#10477" class="InductiveConstructor">sub</a><a id="18176" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18177" class="Argument">v</a> <a id="18179" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18181" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18181" class="Bound">v</a><a id="18182" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18184" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18184" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="18186" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18186" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="18190" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18192" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18192" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a>
    <a id="18200" class="Keyword">with</a> <a id="18205" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#16175" class="Function">↓→𝔼</a> <a id="18209" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18210" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18146" class="Bound">Γ</a><a id="18211" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18213" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18214" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18150" class="Bound">γ</a><a id="18215" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18217" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18218" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18154" class="Bound">γ&#39;</a><a id="18220" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18222" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18223" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18159" class="Bound">M</a><a id="18224" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18226" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18167" class="Bound">𝔾γγ&#39;</a> <a id="18231" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18184" class="Bound">d</a> <a id="18233" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18234" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#4289" class="Function">AboveFun-⊑</a> <a id="18245" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18192" class="Bound">fv&#39;</a> <a id="18249" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18186" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a><a id="18253" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="18255" class="Symbol">...</a> <a id="18259" class="Symbol">|</a> <a id="18261" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18263" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18263" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18265" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18267" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18269" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18269" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="18273" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18275" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18275" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="18278" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18280" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18282" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="18290" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18292" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18263" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="18294" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18296" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟨</a> <a id="18298" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18269" class="Bound">M⇓c</a> <a id="18302" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="18304" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#11036" class="Function">sub-𝕍</a> <a id="18310" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#18275" class="Bound">𝕍v</a> <a id="18313" class="Bound">v&#39;⊑v</a> <a id="18318" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a> <a id="18320" href="https://agda.github.io/agda-stdlib/Agda.Builtin.Sigma.html#139" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">⟩</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

* Case `var`. Looking up `x` in `γ'` yields some closure, `clos M' δ`,
  and from `𝔾 γ γ'` we have `𝔼 (γ x) (clos M' δ)`. With the premise
  `AboveFun (γ x)`, we obtain a closure `c` such that `δ ⊢ M' ⇓ c`
  and `𝕍 (γ x) c`. To conclude `γ' ⊢ x ⇓ c` via `⇓-var`, we 
  need `γ' x ≡ clos M' δ`, which is obvious, but it requires some
  Agda shananigans via the `kth-x` lemma to get our hands on it.

* Case `↦-elim`. We have `γ ⊢ L · M ↓ v`.
  The induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ L ↓ v₁ ↦ v`
  gives us `γ' ⊢ L ⇓ clos L' δ` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`.
  Of course, `L' ≡ ƛ N` for some `N`.
  By the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
  we have `𝔼 v₁ (clos M γ')`.
  Together with the premise `AboveFun v` and `𝕍 v (clos L' δ)`,
  we obtain a closure `c'` such that `δ ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v c'`.
  We conclude that `γ' ⊢ L · M ⇓ c'` by rule `⇓-app`.

* Case `↦-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ v ↦ w`.
  We immediately have `γ' ⊢ ƛ M ⇓ clos (ƛ M) γ'` by rule `⇓-lam`.
  But we also need to prove `𝕍 (v ↦ w) (clos (ƛ N) γ')`.
  Let `c` by an arbitrary closure such that `𝔼 v c`.
  Suppose `v'` is greater than a function value.
  We need to show that `γ' , c ⊢ N ⇓ c'` and `𝕍 v' c'` for some `c'`.
  We prove this by the induction hypothesis for `γ , v ⊢ N ↓ v'`
  but we must first show that `𝔾 (γ , v) (γ' , c)`. We prove
  that by the lemma `𝔾-ext`, using facts `𝔾 γ γ'` and `𝔼 v c`.

* Case `⊥-intro`. We have the premise `AboveFun ⊥`, but that's impossible.

* Case `⊔-intro`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ (v₁ ⊔ v₂)` and `AboveFun (v₁ ⊔ v₂)`
  and need to show `γ' ⊢ M ↓ c` and `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c` for some `c`.
  Again, by `AboveFun-⊔`, at least one of `v₁` or `v₂` is greater than
  a function.

  * Suppose both `v₁` and `v₂` are greater than a function value.
    By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁` and `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₂`
    we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₁`, `𝕍 v₁ c₁`, `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c₂`, and `𝕍 v₂ c₂`
    for some `c₁` and `c₂`. Because `⇓` is deterministic, we have `c₂ ≡ c₁`.
    Then by `𝕍⊔-intro` we conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) c₁`.

  * Without loss of generality, suppose `v₁` is greater than a function
    value but `v₂` is not.  By the induction hypotheses for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v₁`,
    and using `𝕍→WHNF`, we have `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N) γ₁`
    and `𝕍 v₁ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.
    Then because `v₂` is not greater than a function, we also have
    `𝕍 v₂ (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`. We conclude that `𝕍 (v₁ ⊔ v₂) (clos (ƛ N) γ₁)`.
    
* Case `sub`. We have `γ ⊢ M ↓ v`, `v' ⊑ v`, and `AboveFun v'`.
  We need to show that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v' c` for some `c`.
  We have `AboveFun v` by `AboveFun-⊑`,
  so the induction hypothesis for `γ ⊢ M ↓ v` gives us a closure `c`
  such that `γ' ⊢ M ⇓ c` and `𝕍 v c`. We conclude that `𝕍 v' c` by `sub-𝕍`.


## Proof of denotational adequacy

The adequacy property is a corollary of the main lemma.
We have `∅ ⊢ ƛ N ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥`, so `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)`
gives us `∅ ⊢ M ↓ ⊥ ↦ ⊥`. Then the main lemma gives us
`∅ ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) γ` for some `N′` and `γ`.

## Call-by-name equivalent to full beta reduction


[JGS: to do: update this text]


We obtain the other direction through the denotational semantics.
By the soundness result we have `ℰ M ≃ ℰ (ƛ N)`.
Then by adequacy we conclude that `∅' ⊢ M ⇓ clos (ƛ N′) δ`
for some `N′` and `δ`.

             <a id="22141" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2261" class="Function">∅&#39;</a> <a id="22144" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2627" class="Datatype Operator">⊢</a> <a id="22146" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22009" class="Bound">M</a> <a id="22148" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2627" class="Datatype Operator">⇓</a> <a id="22150" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/CallByName.md %}{% raw %}#2082" class="InductiveConstructor">clos</a> <a id="22155" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22156" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Untyped.md %}{% raw %}#4238" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">ƛ</a> <a id="22158" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22091" class="Bound">N′</a><a id="22160" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="22162" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22111" class="Bound">δ</a>
<a id="22164" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21993" class="Function">reduce→cbn</a> <a id="22175" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22175" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a> <a id="22181" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="22183" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#21291" class="Function">adequacy</a> <a id="22192" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="22193" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Soundness.md %}{% raw %}#24644" class="Function">soundness</a> <a id="22203" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link out/plfa/Adequacy.md %}{% raw %}#22175" class="Bound">M—↠ƛN</a><a id="22208" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Putting the two directions of the proof together, we show that
call-by-name evaluation is equivalent to β reduction with respect
to finding weak head normal forms.
